add_namespace = rusfor


country_event = { #Unlock focus tree
	id = rusfor.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1"}
	title = rusfor.1.t
	desc = rusfor.1.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		date > 1937.04.08
		OR = {
			has_war = no
			AND = {
				has_war = yes
				NOT = {
					any_enemy_country = {
						ic_ratio = {
							tag = ROOT
							ratio > 0.3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			country_exists = SOV
			country_exists = SIB
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = unlock_diplomatic_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = unlock_diplomatic
		}
	}


}

country_event = { #Security of the Eastern border OTT
	id = rusfor.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.2"}
	title = rusfor.2.t
	desc = rusfor.2.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = OTT
		is_subject = no
		controls_state = 291
		controls_state = 554
		RUS = { is_subject = no }
		231 = {
			OR = {
				is_controlled_by = RUS
				controller = { is_subject_of = RUS }
			}
		}
		country_exists = EGY
		country_exists = SAU
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = RUS
			is_in_faction_with = RUS
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			is_in_faction_with = EGY
			is_in_faction_with = SAU
			EGY = {
				is_subject_of = OTT
			}
			SAU = {
				is_subject_of = OTT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.2.a #Send the Prince!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = OTT_initiated_NAP_RUS
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.2.b #No deals with the Russians!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_stability = -0.04
	}

}

country_event = { #Nap with Ottomans!
	id = rusfor.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.3"}
	title = rusfor.3.t
	desc = rusfor.3.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.3.a #ok sign it
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = OTT }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = OTT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = OTT
			modifier = OTT_initiated_NAP_RUS
		}
		OTT = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.4
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.3.b #Include armenia in deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 55
		}
		trigger = {
			ARM = {
				is_subject_of = OTT
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		OTT = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.5
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.3.c #No
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_stability = -0.04
	}

}

country_event = { #The Crimea
	id = rusfor.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.7"}
	title = rusfor.7.t
	desc = rusfor.7.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		date > 1938.01.01
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			UKR = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
		}
		UKR = {
			owns_state = 137
			controls_state = 137
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
				is_subject_of = RUS
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 45
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.7.a #Try to lease the Crimea.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_state_core = 137
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = OTT
			modifier = RUS_lease_crimea
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BUL
			modifier = RUS_lease_crimea
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = RUS_lease_crimea
		}
		UKR = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.8
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.7.b #Leave the Crimea for the Ukraine.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = OTT
			modifier = RUS_not_lease_crimea1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = BUL
			modifier = RUS_not_lease_crimea1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = RUS_not_lease_crimea1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = RUS_not_lease_crimea2
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Russia asks to lease the Crimea
	id = rusfor.8
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.8"}
	title = rusfor.8.t
	desc = rusfor.8.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.8.a #Give the Crimea to the Russians.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 137
			send_equipment = {
				target = UKR
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = 2000
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = received_equipment_2000
		random_owned_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		random_owned_state = {
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 2
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_lease_crimea2
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.9
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.8.b #No, the Crimea is Ukrainian now!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				UKR = {
					is_subject_of = RUS
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = UKR
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = UKR
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_refuse_lease_crimea
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.10
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #The Russo-Japanese War MON
	id = rusfor.11
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.11"}
	title = rusfor.11.t
	desc = rusfor.11.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = MON
		date > 1939.01.01
		RUS = {
			has_war_with = JAP
		}
		is_subject = no
		has_war = no
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = QIE
			is_in_faction_with = JAP
			is_in_faction_with = RUS
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 190
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.11.a #We cannot afford to intervene.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.11.b #Attack Russia!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = RUS
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = MON_rusjap_attack_russia1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = QIE
			modifier = MON_rusjap_attack_russia2
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.12
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

		}
		trigger = {

		}

		}

		}

		}
		RUS = {

				id = rusfor.13
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

			factor = 40
		}
		trigger = {

		}

country_event = { #Mongolia attacks Russia! JAP
	id = rusfor.12
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.12"}
	title = rusfor.12.t
	desc = rusfor.12.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.12.a #Add Mongolia to our alliance.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = MON
			modifier = MON_rusjap_ally
		}
		JAP = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "japanese_mongol_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = MON
					}
					JAP = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = MON
					}
					JAP = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
					add_to_faction = MON
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.12.b #no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = MON
			modifier = MON_rusjap_not_ally
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Fate of White Ruthenia
	id = rusfor.16
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.16"}
	title = rusfor.16.t
	desc = rusfor.16.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		owns_state = 206
		owns_state = 207
		controls_state = 206
		controls_state = 207
		NOT = {
			country_exists = WHR
			has_country_flag = RUS_INT_FULLWHR
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 12
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.16.a #Restore White Ruthenia's 1936 borders!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WHR
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					state = 241
					state = 210
					state = 242
					state = 243
				}

			}
			WHR = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusfor.17
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.16.b #Integrate areas with a Russian majority and restore White Ruthenia!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_state_core = 207
		add_state_core = 96
		every_state = {
			limit = {

country_event = { #Minority policies in White Ruthenia
	id = rusfor.19
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.19"}
	title = rusfor.19.t
	desc = rusfor.19.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.19.a #Guarantee wide rights for all minorities in White Ruthenia!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.3
				OR = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -60
		set_country_flag = RUS_minority_right_WHR
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.19.b #Restore Russification policies!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 13
				OR = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		set_country_flag = RUS_russification_WHR
	}

}

country_event = { #Independence of Ukraine
	id = rusfor.23
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.23"}
	title = rusfor.23.t
	desc = rusfor.23.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.23.a #Puppet them!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		puppet = UKR
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = RUS_puppet_ukraine
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				UKR = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = UKR_communist
					NOT = {
						has_government = totalist
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			UKR = {
				drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				UKR = {
					NOT = {
						has_cosmetic_tag = UKR_communist
					}
					OR = {
						has_government = totalist
						has_government = syndicalist
						has_government = radical_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			UKR = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_communist
			}
		}
		UKR = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.24
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.23.b #Full independence!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = RUS_puppet_ukraine1
		}
	}

}

	desc = rusfor.47.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

		tag = RUS
		has_war_with = FRA
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_patriotic_war
			country_exists = SOV
			country_exists = SIB
		}
		is_subject = no
		OR = {
			has_government = social_democrat
			has_government = social_liberal
			has_government = market_liberal
			has_government = social_conservative
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.47.a #We will march through Avenue des Champs-Elysées!
		add_stability = 0.2
		add_war_support = 0.25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = disarmed_nation
			}
			remove_ideas = disarmed_nation
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = volunteer_only
			}
			remove_ideas = volunteer_only
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = limited_conscription
			}
			remove_ideas = limited_conscription
			add_ideas = extensive_conscription
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_patriotic_war
	}

}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.68"}
	title = rusfor.68.t
	desc = rusfor.68.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.68.a #We shall wipe Mongolia from the map!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		add_state_core = 563
		add_state_core = 564
		add_state_core = 811
		add_state_core = 654
		declare_war_on = {
			target = MON
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.68.b #Evacuate all Russian citizens from Mongolia and seal the border.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_SIB_PANIC
		add_stability = -0.2
	}

}

country_event = { #Urga Has Fallen!
	id = rusfor.70
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.70"}
	title = rusfor.70.t
	desc = rusfor.70.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		country_exists = MON
		has_war_with = MON
		controls_state = 330
		controls_state = 564
		controls_state = 811
		MON = {
			is_subject = no
			is_in_faction = no
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 3
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.70.a #Offer them protectorate status
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		add_state_core = 563
		add_state_core = 564
		add_state_core = 811
		add_state_core = 654
		MON = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.75
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_SIB_PANIC
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.70.b #Make an example out of them, unconditional surrender!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		clr_country_flag = RUS_SIB_PANIC
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = DKB
			modifier = RUS_mon_unconditional_surrender1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ALO
			modifier = RUS_mon_unconditional_surrender1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = TRK
			modifier = RUS_mon_unconditional_surrender1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = RUS_mon_unconditional_surrender2
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Mongols Accept!
	id = rusfor.71
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.71"}
	title = rusfor.71.t
	desc = rusfor.71.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.71.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				MON = {
					owns_state = 329
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.76
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		puppet = MON
		if = {
			limit = {
				SIK = {
					is_subject_of = MON
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = SIK
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				XSM = {
					is_subject_of = MON
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = XSM
			}
		}
		MON = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.73
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = TIB
			}
			TIB = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.72
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Urga Captured MON
	id = rusfor.75
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.75"}
	title = rusfor.75.t
	desc = rusfor.75.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.75.a #We have no choice but to submit...
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		RUS = {
			white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = no
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 563
					state = 564
					state = 811
					state = 654
				}
			}
			RUS = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		#set_country_flag = Ungern_Dead
		remove_state_core = 563
		remove_state_core = 564
		remove_state_core = 811
		remove_state_core = 654
		remove_state_claim = 572
		remove_state_claim = 653
		remove_state_claim = 580
		remove_state_claim = 579
		remove_state_claim = 590
		remove_state_claim = 588
		remove_state_claim = 403
		remove_state_claim = 571
		remove_state_claim = 570
		remove_state_claim = 578
		remove_state_claim = 40
		remove_state_claim = 569
		remove_state_claim = 568
		remove_state_claim = 567
		remove_state_claim = 566
		remove_state_claim = 577
		remove_state_claim = 516
		remove_state_claim = 576
		remove_state_claim = 575

		remove_state_claim = 565
		remove_state_claim = 561
		remove_state_claim = 657
		remove_state_claim = 560
		remove_state_claim = 574
		remove_state_claim = 644
		remove_state_claim = 562
		remove_state_claim = 637
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.71
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.75.b #The Baron shall lead us to victory or death!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.74
			}
		}
	}

}

		tag = RUS

country_event = { #The Cossacks Resolve
	id = rusfor.85
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.85"}
	title = rusfor.85.t
	desc = rusfor.85.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.85.a
		puppet = DKB
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = DKB
			modifier = RUS_puppet_route_caucasus
		}
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "great_russian_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = DKB
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = DKB
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = DKB
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #The leasing of port arthur
	id = rusfor.98
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.98"}
	title = rusfor.98.t
	desc = rusfor.98.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			328 = {
				is_core_of = RUS
			}
		}
		OR = {
			745 = {
				owner = {
					is_subject_of = RUS
					controls_state = 745
				}
			}
			AND = {
				controls_state = 745
				328 = {
					controller = {
						is_subject_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 5
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.98.a #lease the porth arthur
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		add_state_core = 745
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = RUS
				OR = {
					controls_state = 745
					controls_state = 328
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.99
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = RUS
				modifier = RUS_lease_port_arthur
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.98.b #leave the port arthur for china
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 745
				controls_state = 745
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = RUS
					controls_state = 328
				}
				transfer_state = 745
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 745
				}
				controls_state = 745
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_subject_of = RUS
					controls_state = 328
				}
				set_state_controller = 745
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = RUS
				OR = {
					controls_state = 745
					controls_state = 328
				}
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = RUS
				modifier = RUS_not_lease_port_arthur
			}
		}
	}

}

					NOT = {
						controls_state = 10
					}
					NOT = {
						owns_state = 10
					}
					POL = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 10
						}
					}
					POL = {
						NOT = {
							owns_state = 10
						}
					}
					10 = {
						is_core_of = RUS
					}
					AND = {
						country_exists = POL
						NOT = {
							POL = {
								is_subject_of = RUS
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.2111 days = 100
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Status of Poland
	id = rusfor.115
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.115"}
	title = rusfor.115.t
	desc = rusfor.115.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
		has_global_flag = RUS_independent_POL
		POL = {
			owns_state = 10
			controls_state = 10
			is_subject_of = RUS
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 100
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.115.a #Poland remains independent
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = RUS_let_poland_independent
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.115.b #integrate poland
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = RUS_reintegrate_poland
		}
		POL = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.117
			}
		}
	}

}

	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				POL = {
					owns_state = 10
					controls_state = 10
					is_subject_of = RUS
				}
				NOT = {
					10 = {
						is_core_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.121
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					POL = {
						NOT = {
							controls_state = 10
						}
					}
					POL = {
						NOT = {
							owns_state = 10
						}
					}
					10 = {
						is_core_of = RUS
					}
					NOT = {
						POL = {
							is_subject_of = RUS
						}
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.2120 days = 100
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #GER Russia demands concessions in the Caucasus
	id = rusfor.1048
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1048"}
	title = rusfor.1048.t
	desc = rusfor.1048.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1048.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		RUS = {
			clr_country_flag = RUS_GER_blocks_caucasus
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_accept_concession_caucasus
		add_stability = -0.04
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = GER_accepted_concessions_RUS1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = DKB
			modifier = GER_accepted_concessions_RUS2
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AZB
			modifier = GER_accepted_concessions_RUS2
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = DKB }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = DKB
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = AZB }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = AZB
				relation = guarantee
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DKB = {
					is_subject_of = GER
				}
			}
			end_puppet = DKB
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AZB = {
					is_subject_of = GER
				}
			}
			end_puppet = AZB
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = RUS }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = RUS
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DKB = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			DKB = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1050 days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AZB = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
			AZB = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1051 days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				DKB = {
					is_subject = no
				}
				country_exists = DKB
			}
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1053 days = 4
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				AZB = {
					is_subject = no
				}
				country_exists = AZB
			}
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1054 days = 4
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1048.b #Never!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1049
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = GER_refused_concessions_RUS2
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = DKB
			modifier = GER_refused_concessions_RUS1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AZB
			modifier = GER_refused_concessions_RUS1

country_event = { #Iran accepts!
	id = rusfor.1067

	title = rusfor.1067.t

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1067.a #Hurray!
		add_stability = 0.06
		give_guarantee = PER
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "russo_persian_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = PER
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = PER
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = PER
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

				create_faction = "sino_russian_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					QIE = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					QIE = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = QIE
					}
					add_to_faction = RUS
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1080.b #No, we cannot trust the Russians!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_ally_china_declined
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Japan demands NAP
	id = rusfor.1110
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1110"}
	title = rusfor.1110.t
	desc = rusfor.1110.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1110.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 745
		}
		JAP = {
			remove_state_core = 745
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = RUS_agreed_manchuria
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = JAP }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = JAP
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1111
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1110.b #who do they think they are? claim manchuria too!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 45
		}
		add_stability = 0.02

		# Re-instate the Manchurian claims
		add_state_claim = 714
		add_state_claim = 715
		add_state_claim = 716
		add_state_claim = 717
		add_state_claim = 328
		add_state_claim = 884
		add_state_claim = 883
		add_state_claim = 885
		add_state_claim = 886
		add_state_claim = 610
		set_global_flag = RUS_jap_denied_first_agreement_manchuria
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1099
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1110.c #we won't reach to an agreement
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = RUS_back_down_manchuria
		}
		add_stability = -0.04
	}

}

country_event = { #Russia offers us an alliance!
	id = rusfor.1117
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1117"}
	title = rusfor.1117.t
	desc = rusfor.1117.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1117.a #Join them!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "inter_steppe_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = MON
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = MON
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = MON
				}
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = MON
			modifier = RUS_MON_accepted_alliance
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1117.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = MON
			modifier = RUS_MON_declined_alliance
		}
	}

}

		name = rusfor.1122.a #Accept their offer.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		add_to_faction = PLC
		add_stability = -0.02
		PLC = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.11231
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = POL_join_mitteleuropa_rusee
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PLC
			modifier = POL_join_mitteleuropa_rusee2
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1122.b #Just guarantee
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = PLC }
			give_guarantee = PLC
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PLC
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = GER_guarantee_poland_rusee2
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = PLC
			modifier = GER_guarantee_poland_rusee1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1122.c #Stable relationship with Russia is more important.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = GER_refuse_poland_rusee1
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = POL
			modifier = GER_refuse_poland_rusee2
		}
	}

}

				target = PLC

			}

country_event = { #The Second Weltkrieg
	id = rusfor.1124
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1124"}
	title = rusfor.1124.t
	desc = rusfor.1124.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1124.a #We must join arms with the Internationale!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				controls_state = 16
				is_subject = no
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = totalist
			}
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_internationale1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = NFA
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_internationale1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_internationale2
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SRI
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_internationale3
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ENG
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_internationale4
		}
		add_stability = -0.06
		FRA = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1125
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1124.e #Demand concessions in Eastern Europe!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
			OR = {
				BAT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				WHR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				UKR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}

			GER = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
				controls_state = 64
				is_subject = no
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = totalist
				}
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = RUS_WKII_demand_concessions
		}
		add_stability = 0.06

		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1155
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1124.f #We must join arms with the Entente!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			CAN = {
				has_war_with = FRA
				is_faction_leader = yes
				controls_state = 276
				is_subject = no
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = totalist
				}
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_entente1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_entente2
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = SRI
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_entente3
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ENG
			modifier = RUS_WKII_join_entente4
		}
		add_stability = -0.06
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					CAN = {
						is_in_faction_with = GBR
					}
				}
			}
			CAN = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1127
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAN = {
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
				}
			}
			GBR = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1128
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1124.g #A perfect chance to reclaim our lost territories from the Völkerbund!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {

			GER = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			OR = {
				FIN = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				UKR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				WHR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
				OR = {
					BAT = {
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
					AND = {
						EST = {
							exists = yes
							is_in_faction_with = GER
						}
						LAT = {
							exists = yes
							is_in_faction_with = GER
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.06
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = RUS_WKII_reclaimed_territories
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = GER
			type = annex_everything
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_WKII_reclaimed_territories
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1124.h #Try to make a deal with the devil!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				has_war_with = GER
				controls_state = 16
				is_subject = no
			}
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = totalist
				}
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
				is_in_faction_with = CAN
				is_in_faction_with = USA
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = RUS_WKII_deal_devil1
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = RUS_WKII_deal_devil2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = RUS
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = RUS
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		FRA = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1133
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1124.i #A perfect chance to reclaim lost territories from the Internationale!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			FRA = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			OR = {
				WHR = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
				UKR = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
				FIN = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
				OR = {
					BAT = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
					}
					AND = {
						EST = {
							exists = yes
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
						}
						LAT = {
							exists = yes
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.06
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FRA
			modifier = RUS_WKII_reclaimed_territories
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FRA
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	title = rusfor.1135.t
	desc = rusfor.1135.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1135.a #We have no choice.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		add_stability = 0.2
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1137
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1135.b #Resist them
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction = yes
				NOT = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction_with = WHR
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
				remove_from_faction = WHR
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			dismantle_faction = yes
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1138 days = 1
			}
		}
	}

}

		has_country_flag = RUS_EXP

			controls_state = 206
			is_subject_of = RUS
		}
	}

	}

country_event = { #hidden event to check integration WHR
	id = rusfor.11531
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.11531"}
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.11531.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				WHR = {
					controls_state = 206
					owns_state = 206
				}
				NOT = {
					206 = {
						is_core_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1153
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						WHR = {
							controls_state = 206
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						WHR = {
							owns_state = 206
						}
					}
					206 = {
						is_core_of = RUS
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.11531 days = 100
			}
		}
	}

}

				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = UKR
					}

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {

						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = UKR

					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = UKR
				}
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = UKR
			modifier = RUS_ally_syndie_ukraine_accept
		}
	}

			}
		}

		}

			ROM = {

				}
			}

					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.06
		RUS = {

				id = rusfor.1182
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Romanian proposal
	id = rusfor.1182
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1182"}
	title = rusfor.1182.t
	desc = rusfor.1182.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1182.a #Accept their terms
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = radical_socialist
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		ROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1183
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_ally
		}
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "volga_danubian_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROM
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = ROM
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = ROM
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1182.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		ROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1184
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_refused
		}
	}

}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			ROM = {
				is_subject = no
			}
			} #Have to disable it if you brought aid to monarchists
		ROM = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1199
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = ROM
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_support_side
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1190.c #This is a perfect chance to gain control over Romania!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = ROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RRM
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

country_event = { #Russian offer RRM
	id = rusfor.1191
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1191"}
	title = rusfor.1191.t
	desc = rusfor.1191.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1191.a #Accept their proposition
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 65
		}
		trigger = {
			RUS = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1192
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_accept_support
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1191.b #we need such an ally
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		trigger = {
			RUS = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = GER
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1193
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_accept_support
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1191.c #Never! We don't sell our land!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_RRM_refuse_support
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_refused_support
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_ROM_refuse_support
			}
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1206
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_ROM_refuse_support
				}
			}
			RUS = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.1198
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Alliance with Romania
	id = rusfor.1192
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1192"}
	title = rusfor.1192.t
	desc = rusfor.1192.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1192.a
		set_country_flag = RUS_RRM_bess
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RRM
			modifier = RUS_claim_bessarabia_ally_cw
		}
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "volga_danubian_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = RRM
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = RRM
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = RRM
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Bessarabia question
	id = rusfor.1195
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1195"}
	title = rusfor.1195.t
	desc = rusfor.1195.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RRM
		RUS = {
			has_country_flag = RUS_RRM_bess
		}
		controls_state = 78
		NOT = {
			country_exists = ROM
			has_war_with = HUN
			has_war_with = AUS
			has_war_with = BUL
			has_war_with = OTT
			has_war_with = POL
		}
		} #must add AH and commonwealth

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1195.a #Secede Bessarabia to Russia
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		remove_state_core = 192
		remove_state_core = 791
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 78
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 192
			}
			RUS = {
				transfer_state = 192
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 791
			}
			RUS = {
				transfer_state = 791
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1196
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1195.b #No, we will fight for our land!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1197
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = RUS
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
					is_in_faction_with = RRM
				}
				remove_from_faction = RRM
			}
		}
	}

}

	desc = rusfor.1208.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1208.a #We shall seize and convert all of the ships in the harbour!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = RUS_TRM_NAVY_BIG
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_trmnavunits_tt
		}
		add_political_power = -80
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = convoy_1
			amount = 50
			producer = RUS
		}
		408 = {
			remove_building = {
				type = industrial_complex level = 2
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = JAP
			modifier = RUS_vladivostok_big
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SOV
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = SOV_TRM_NAVY_BIG
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_trmnavunits_tt
			408 = {
				add_building_construction = {
					type = coastal_bunker
					level = 2
					province = 957

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1220"}
	title = rusfor.1220.t
	desc = rusfor.1220.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1220.a #then it's war
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 98
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = AUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1220.b #back down
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 2
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = AUS
			modifier = RUS_ultimatum_galicia_back_down
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Ultimatum for Galicia puppet of POL
	id = rusfor.1224
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1224"}
	title = rusfor.1224.t
	desc = rusfor.1224.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1224.a #Accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 35
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		RUS = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = POL
				modifier = RUS_ultimatum_galicia_accept
			}
		}
		remove_state_core = 80
		remove_state_core = 88
		remove_state_core = 89
		remove_state_core = 91
		GAL = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1228
			}
		}
		end_puppet = GAL
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = GAL
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			remove_from_faction = GAL
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1224.b #refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		RUS = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = POL
				modifier = RUS_ultimatum_galicia_refuse
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1226
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1224.c #Pre-emptive strike
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		RUS = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = POL
				modifier = RUS_ultimatum_galicia_refuse
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {

country_event = { #Russian claims FIN
	id = rusfor.1229
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1229"}
	title = rusfor.1229.t
	desc = rusfor.1229.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {

			factor = 95
		}

			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1230
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1229.b #All right.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_stability = -0.3
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 146
			transfer_state = 147
			transfer_state = 213
			transfer_state = 215
			transfer_state = 722
			transfer_state = 216
		}
		remove_state_core = 146
		remove_state_core = 147
		remove_state_core = 213
		remove_state_core = 215
		remove_state_core = 722
		remove_state_core = 216
		custom_effect_tooltip = received_equipment_5000
		random_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				free_building_slots = {
					building = industrial_complex
					size > 0
					include_locked = yes
				}
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1231
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Finland refused!
	id = rusfor.1230
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1230"}
	title = rusfor.1230.t
	desc = rusfor.1230.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1230.a #Take it back by force!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}

		GER = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = FIN }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = FIN
					relation = guarantee
					active = no
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FIN
			modifier = RUS_crush_finland
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = GER
			modifier = RUS_crush_finland
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FIN
			type = annex_everything
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1230.b #Forget about it.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		add_stability = -0.06
	}

}

country_event = { #Transfer of the territory
	id = rusfor.1231
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1231"}
	title = rusfor.1231.t
	desc = rusfor.1231.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1231.a #Another victory for Russian diplomacy!
		add_stability = 0.1
		set_country_flag = RUS_fin_accepted_demand_karelia
		give_guarantee = FIN
		send_equipment = {
			target = FIN
			type = infantry_equipment
			amount = 5000
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = FIN }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = FIN
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		FIN = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = RUS }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = RUS
					relation = non_aggression_pact
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #We've been defeated! FIN
	id = rusfor.1232
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1232"}
	title = rusfor.1232.t
	desc = rusfor.1232.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FIN
		is_subject = no
		NOT = {
			is_in_faction_with = CSA
			is_in_faction_with = GER
			is_in_faction_with = FRA
		}
		has_war_with = RUS
		RUS = {
			OR = {
				controls_state = 840
				AND = {
					controls_state = 146
					controls_state = 215
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1232.a #Sue for peace!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		add_stability = -0.04
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1233
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1232.b #We can still win this!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_stability = -0.08
	}

}

country_event = { #Russia offers us an alliance! FIN
	id = rusfor.1236
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1236"}
	title = rusfor.1236.t
	desc = rusfor.1236.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1236.a #Join them!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "finno_russian_coalition"
				add_to_faction = FIN
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				add_to_faction = FIN
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = FIN
				}
			}
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_FIN_accepted_alliance
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1236.b #Refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_FIN_declined_alliance
		}
	}

}

			}
		}

			factor = 5

				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_DEM_REP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_DEM_REP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 7
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_VLA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_VLA
			}

					has_country_flag = RUS_ARI_REP
					has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_DMI
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_MIL_DICT
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 6
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_MIL_DICT
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_vozhd
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 18
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_vozhd
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = RUS_ai_choose_new_alliance
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1237.e #We don't need any allies, we shall stay out of global affairs.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_DEM_REP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_DEM_REP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_VLA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_VLA
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_ARI_REP
					has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_DMI
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_ARI_REP
					has_country_flag = RUS_TSAR_DMI
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_MIL_DICT
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_MIL_DICT
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				has_country_flag = RUS_vozhd
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.2
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
				has_country_flag = RUS_vozhd
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = syndicalist
				has_government = totalist
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = RUS_DEM_REP
				}

		if = {

				has_country_flag = RUS_DEM_REP

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1237.f #We will fight for a better world with the Commune of France!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 15
				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 12
				has_country_flag = RUS_EXP
			}

			}

	}

			factor = 5

				has_country_flag = RUS_REAL

	}

country_event = { #Russia wants to join the Entente CAN - not wrangel
	id = rusfor.1238
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1238"}
	title = rusfor.1238.t
	desc = rusfor.1238.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1238.a #Yes, let them join!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 94
		}
		add_to_faction = RUS
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_join_entente
		}
		RUS = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = RUS_join_entente
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.06
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1239
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1238.b #We'd rather not.
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_join_entente_refused
		}
		RUS = {
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				target = CAN
				modifier = RUS_join_entente_refused
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1238.c #How about signing a non-aggression pact instead?
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1243
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Canadians propose a non-aggression pact
	id = rusfor.1243
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1243"}
	title = rusfor.1243.t
	desc = rusfor.1243.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1243.a #If it's all you can offer...
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = CAN
			modifier = RUS_join_entente_NAP
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = CAN }
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = CAN
				relation = non_aggression_pact
			}
		}
		CAN = {
			if = {
				limit = { country_exists = RUS }
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = RUS
					relation = non_aggression_pact
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1243.b #no means no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
	}

}

country_event = { #New Global Alliance?
	id = rusfor.1250
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1250"}
	title = rusfor.1250.t
	desc = rusfor.1250.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1250.a #Search for allies in Pacific region!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			country_exists = JAP
			JAP = {
				is_subject = no
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = RUS
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = totalist
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1251 days = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1250.b #search for allies in europe!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = SER
					SER = {
						is_subject = no
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_in_faction_with = CAN
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
							has_war_with = RUS
							has_government = syndicalist
							has_government = totalist
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = YUG
					YUG = {
						is_subject = no
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_in_faction_with = CAN
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
							has_war_with = RUS
							has_government = syndicalist
							has_government = totalist
						}
					}
				}
				AND = {
					country_exists = AUS
					AUS = {
						owns_state = 102
						controls_state = 102
						owns_state = 9
						controls_state = 9
						is_subject = no
						NOT = {
							is_in_faction_with = GER
							is_in_faction_with = CAN
							is_in_faction_with = RUS
							is_in_faction_with = JAP
							is_in_faction_with = FRA
							has_war_with = RUS
							has_government = syndicalist
							has_government = totalist
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = rusfor.1254 days = 1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1250.c #create a completely new alliance!
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_rule = {
			can_create_factions = yes
		}
	}

}

country_event = { #Alliance with Russia? JAP
	id = rusfor.1251
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1251"}
	title = rusfor.1251.t
	desc = rusfor.1251.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1251.a #yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "eurasian_alliance"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = JAP
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1252
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_ally_japan_focus
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1251.b #no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = RUS_ally_japan_focus_refuse
		}
	}

}

		}

country_event = { #New power in Europe
	id = rusfor.1256
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rusfor.1256"}
	title = rusfor.1256.t
	desc = rusfor.1256.d
	#picture = GFX_petain_NFA

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1256.a
		add_stability = 0.06
		RUS = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
				create_faction = "slavic_brothers"
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = SER
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = SER
					}
					RUS = { add_to_faction = PREV }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						is_in_faction = yes
						NOT = {
							is_faction_leader = yes
						}
					}
				}
				every_other_country = {
					limit = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction_with = RUS
					}
					add_to_faction = SER
				}
			}
		}
	}

}

		name = rusfor.1266.a #Invite the Russians to protect and develop White Ruthenia.

			factor = 70
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				WHR = {
					OR = {
						is_subject_of = GER
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}

			GER = {
				country_event = {
					id = rusfor.12722
				}
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_autonomy = { target = WHR autonomy_state = autonomy_free }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				RUS = { puppet = WHR }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			leave_faction = yes
		}
		separate_peace_all_wars = yes

		RUS = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1267
			}
		}

		204 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		206 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		207 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = rusfor.1266.b #Maybe the Germans will help us

			factor = 25
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = GER

			}
		}

		add_stability = 0.04

		GER = {
			country_event = {
				id = rusfor.1269
			}
		}
	}

		}
